      • addLocalTaxCode

        public void addLocalTaxCode(java.lang.CharSequence param)
        Appends the specified LocalTaxCode to the end of the collection.
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Local Tax Code user for Local Tax. Automatically updated by the system from COUPON.TAX.CODE file. This field could be populated with a TAX ID or a TAX.TYPE.CONDITION ID. If a TAX Id is used and the TAX record has the field LINK.TAX populated then all taxes linked to the Id enteredwill be displayed using the multi-values as required, the associated percentages will be displayed in the fieldLOCAL.TAX.PERC. If APPL.GEN.CONDITION application has a record with id DIARY, then CONTRACT.GRP is identified based on theconditions defined in the fields from DECIS.FIELD to DECISION.TO in APPL.GEN.CONDITION. In TAX.TYPE.CONDITION, thetax codes that are assigned to particular groups of contract (CONTRACT.GRP) are populated in this field. Validation Rules: Either a valid TAX Or a Valid TAX.TYPE.CONDITION Only multi-value 1 may be used for entry

        Parameters:
        param - the LocalTaxCode to append
        Returns:
        nothing

      • addLocalTaxCode

        public void addLocalTaxCode(TField param)
        Appends the specified LocalTaxCode to the end of the collection.
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Local Tax Code user for Local Tax. Automatically updated by the system from COUPON.TAX.CODE file. This field could be populated with a TAX ID or a TAX.TYPE.CONDITION ID. If a TAX Id is used and the TAX record has the field LINK.TAX populated then all taxes linked to the Id enteredwill be displayed using the multi-values as required, the associated percentages will be displayed in the fieldLOCAL.TAX.PERC. If APPL.GEN.CONDITION application has a record with id DIARY, then CONTRACT.GRP is identified based on theconditions defined in the fields from DECIS.FIELD to DECISION.TO in APPL.GEN.CONDITION. In TAX.TYPE.CONDITION, thetax codes that are assigned to particular groups of contract (CONTRACT.GRP) are populated in this field. Validation Rules: Either a valid TAX Or a Valid TAX.TYPE.CONDITION Only multi-value 1 may be used for entry

        Parameters:
        param - the LocalTaxCode to append
        Returns:
        nothing

      • addStmtNos

        public void addStmtNos(TField param)
        Appends the specified StmtNos to the end of the collection.
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: This field is used by the system in the update of the STATEMENT.NO field. As the STATEMENT.NO field is sub.valued and contain more than one set of entries - as there may be more than onedepository - this field is used in the call to Accounting to hold the STMT.ENTRY and CATEG.ENTRY IDs used in thepostings of the Nostro amount and Reallowance amount. The system automatically moves the contents of this fieldform this field to the relevent position in the STATEMENT.NOS field and is then cleared and therefore will normallybe blank. Technical note : this is done in the program SC.ENT.ACCOUNTING. Validation Rules: This is a NOINPUT field, for internal system use only.

        Parameters:
        param - the StmtNos to append
        Returns:
        nothing

      • getAutoConversion

        public TField getAutoConversion()
        Returns the AutoConversion

        Field description: Enables the automatic settlement of unsettled transactions in the original security, while processing corporate events where one security is being converted to another. Validation Rules: Input allowed only if field ACTUAL.SETTLEMENT is set to YES in SC.PARAMETER. Input allowed only for Stock Conversion Events. Allowed values are Yes,NO and Null. NO and Null are treated differently. NO indicates Auto Conversion is not required.Null indicates,the system should look for a parameter at a higher level i.e AUTO.CONVERSION field in CUSTOMER.SECURITY.

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        TField - The AutoConversion

      • getAutoProcContra

        public TField getAutoProcContra()
        Returns the AutoProcContra

        Field description: Enables the automatic settlement of the Contra settlement record generated for closing out the stock position in the old security while processing corporate events where one security is being converted to another.The settlement records are generated after authorisation of the entitlement.       • getExDate

        public TField getExDate()
        Returns the ExDate

        Field description: The Ex.Div date of the DIARY. All holders in the Security specified as of this date are entitled to the event. When calculating the holding of a particular security position that qualifies for the Corporate Action event thesystem calculates the balance of the security position on this date. All security movements that have a trade datebefore this date are included, all security movements with a trade date equal to or after this date are ignoredwhen calculating the qualifying balnce. Validation Rules: Mandatory input of Standard T24 Date format.

        public TField getLinkImpactAdjust()
        Returns the LinkImpactAdjust

        Field description: Field to define Adjustment on Qualify Holding for Entitlements based on other transactions. Allowed values : BUY,SELL,BOTH BUY - Qualify Holding of current entitlement is based on Qualify Holding calculated based on LINK.IMPACT.VALUE and BUY transactions after the LINK.DIARY.ID that are eligible based on EX / RECORD Date in this event. SELL - Qualify Holding of current entitlement is based on Qualify Holding calculated based on LINK.IMPACT.VALUE and SELL transactions after the LINK.DIARY.ID that are eligible based on EX / RECORD Date in this event. BOTH - Qualify Holding of current entitlement is based on Qualify Holding calculated based on LINK.IMPACT.VALUE and BOTH transactions after the LINK.DIARY.ID that are eligible based on EX / RECORD Date in this event.

      • getNetCharges

        public TField getNetCharges()
        Returns the NetCharges

        Field description: Flag to indicate whether the event is net (free) of charges. This field will dictate the way in which the foreigncharges tax on foreign charges affects the TOTAL.CASH field on the depositories. This flag does not in any wayalter the amount due to the customer. Whether or not the foreign charges tax on the foreign charges are to bededucted from the customer amount is decided by the RATE.TYPE field. Validation Rules: Only input of Y or NO allowed. If the field is set to Y foreign charges tax on foreign charges will be included in the TOTAL.CASH figureassociated with the depository. If the field is set to NO foreign charges tax on foreign charges will not be included in the TOTAL.CASH fieldassociated with the depository. Will default to NO if no input is made.

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        TField - The NetCharges

      • getRetainOption

        public TField getRetainOption()
        Returns the RetainOption

        Field description: When this field is set to YES those Entitlements in which option is chose will be retained on rerunning thecorporate action service. If the qualifying nominal is not changed and it is mandatory event then the newly created entitlement recordwill be defaulted with the nominalopted by the user. If the qualifying nominal is changed and it is a mandatory event, then the freshly created entitlement will beupdated with new qualifyingnominal and the same will be defaulted in option nominal. In the above 2 cases the entitlement will be created in INAU status. If qualifying nominal is changed and partial option is chose then the entitlement will be generated in IHLDstatus without consideringoptions elected by the user in this case user have to re-elect the options. However if the qualifying nominal is not changed and partial option is opted then the newly created entitlementrecord will hold theoptions that were opted by the user and the record will be in INAU status. Validation Rules Allowed values are YES/Null only.

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        TField - The RetainOption

      • getTradeOrValue

        public TField getTradeOrValue()
        Returns the TradeOrValue

        Field description: This field should be used to generate Entitlements based on Value Date. For a Value Date based Entitlement, allSecurity movements that have a Value Date before the EX.DIV date of the DIARY will be included. All positions werethe EX.DIV Date is lesser than the Value Date will be ignored. If this field is left blank, the System will default to the TRADE.OR.VALUE field of the SECURITY.MASTER of theSecurity processed. Validation Rules: Optional Input. Input can be TRADE or VALUE or left Blank.

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        TField - The TradeOrValue

      • getUnfrankedCfiRate

        public TField getUnfrankedCfiRate()
        Returns the UnfrankedCfiRate

        Field description: This field will hold Conduit Foreign Income rate and should not exceed the unfranked rate. This will be a Rate or a Percentage of face value, based on whether field PERCENTAGE is set as No or Yes Validation Rules Field can be inputted only when 1. CASH field for the record in DIARY.TYPE table is set to yes 2. BOND.OR.SHARE set as 'S' in SECURITY.MASTER record 3. FRANKING.CR.ALLOWED field should be set as YES at Parameter level 4. Only when Unfranked rate is inputted Negative rates are not allowed.

      • getUnfrankedRate

        public TField getUnfrankedRate()
        Returns the UnfrankedRate

        Field description: This field will hold the Unfranked rate This will be a Rate or a Percentage of face value, based on whether field PERCENTAGE is set as No or Yes If not available, this will default to the dividend rate minus FRANKED.CREDIT.RATE Validation Rules Field can be inputted only when 1. CASH field for the record in DIARY.TYPE table is set to yes 2. BOND.OR.SHARE set as 'S' in SECURITY.MASTER record 3. FRANKING.CR.ALLOWED field should be set as YES at Parameter level Negative rates are not allowed. Sum of franked credit rate and unfranked rate should be equal to the rate field.

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        TField - The UnfrankedRate

      • getUpfrontPayment

        public TField getUpfrontPayment()
        Returns the UpfrontPayment

        Field description: Field to identify if payment is required prior to security movement. If the flag is set to YES , First Authorisation of ENTITLEMENT will debit customer account and second/Consequentauthorisation of ENTITLEMENT will perform security movement.Otherwise , Authorisation of ENTITLEMENT will perform security movement. UPFRONT.PAYMENT criteria follows below logic: If UPFRONT.PAYMENT field in DIARY.TYPE is not YES or DIARY is NO then event is not eligible for upfront payment If UPFRONT.PAYMENT field in DIARY.TYPE is YES and SC.PARAMETER is NO and DIARY is blank then event is noteligible for upfront payment All other cases apart from above are eligible for upfront payment. Validation Rules Input Allowed- YES,NO

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        TField - The UpfrontPayment

      • getValueDate

        public TField getValueDate()
        Returns the ValueDate

        Field description: Date the portfolios (SEC.ACC.MASTER and related cash accounts) are to be updated by the event. This is the value date of the corporate action event in respect of updating the ACCOUNT and SECURITY.POSITIONfiles as a result of the corporate action. In some cases, it may be found necessary to delay the value date forwhich customers accounts receive value. Such instances may, for example, include those cases where the dividend isreceived by cheque and, should this be in a foreign currency, will require sending for collection. If no date is entered then this field will default to the same date as that entered into the PAY.DATE field. Validation Rules: Mandatory input of Standard T24 Date format.

        Parameters:
        Returns:
        TField - The ValueDate

        public TField getVaultUpdate()

        Field description: YES/NO flag controlling whether a VAULT.EXPECT record will be generated by the Corporate ACtion. Defaults to YES.If the Vault is switched off or the depository is not on VAULT.PARAMETER as being one that updates VAULT.CONTROLthen no VAULT.EXPECT record will be produced even if this field has a value of YES. Will be NO if no Securities are updated by the Corporate Action. Validation Rules: Allowed values are YES/NO only. Mandatory input. Defaulting dependant on the VAULT.PARAMETER file and theDIARY.TYPE record linked to the DIARY record.

        Field description: Local Tax Code user for Local Tax. Automatically updated by the system from COUPON.TAX.CODE file. This field could be populated with a TAX ID or a TAX.TYPE.CONDITION ID. If a TAX Id is used and the TAX record has the field LINK.TAX populated then all taxes linked to the Id enteredwill be displayed using the multi-values as required, the associated percentages will be displayed in the fieldLOCAL.TAX.PERC. If APPL.GEN.CONDITION application has a record with id DIARY, then CONTRACT.GRP is identified based on theconditions defined in the fields from DECIS.FIELD to DECISION.TO in APPL.GEN.CONDITION. In TAX.TYPE.CONDITION, thetax codes that are assigned to particular groups of contract (CONTRACT.GRP) are populated in this field. Validation Rules: Either a valid TAX Or a Valid TAX.TYPE.CONDITION Only multi-value 1 may be used for entry

        Returns:

        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Enables the automatic settlement of unsettled transactions in the original security, while processing corporate events where one security is being converted to another. Validation Rules: Input allowed only if field ACTUAL.SETTLEMENT is set to YES in SC.PARAMETER. Input allowed only for Stock Conversion Events. Allowed values are Yes,NO and Null. NO and Null are treated differently. NO indicates Auto Conversion is not required.Null indicates,the system should look for a parameter at a higher level i.e AUTO.CONVERSION field in CUSTOMER.SECURITY.

        value - The value to set

        public void setBlockPosition(TField value)
        Set the specified value for BlockPosition
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Specifies whether the Security Position updated by the execution of the Corporate Action will be blocked. If the position is to be blocked it can take place at the authorisation of the DIARY record (value DIARY) whenthe entitlements are created unauthorised, or when individual entitlements are authorised (value ENTITLEMENT). Thedefault value for this field is contained in the DIARY.TYPE record. The blocked amount is always theQUALIFY.HOLDING on the ENTITLEMENT record. Blocks are created in the SC.BLOCK.SEC.POS application automaticallywhen a block is required, similarly they are unblocked using the same application automatically. A block / unblockis created under the following circumstances: Position can also be blocked during the election of option in ENTITLEMENT record. This is possible whenBLOCK.POSITION is set as OPTION A value of NONE can be entered to suppress any default option if required. Validation Rules: Optional Input Values DIARY or ENTITLEMENT or NONE or OPTION allowed

If a TAX Id is used and the TAX record has the field LINK.TAX populated then all taxes linked to the Id enteredwill be displayed using the multi-values as required, the associated percentages will be displayed in the fieldLOCAL.TAX.PERC. If APPL.GEN.CONDITION application has a record with id DIARY, then CONTRACT.GRP is identified based on theconditions defined in the fields from DECIS.FIELD to DECISION.TO in APPL.GEN.CONDITION. In TAX.TYPE.CONDITION, thetax codes that are assigned to particular groups of contract (CONTRACT.GRP) are populated in this field. Validation Rules: Either a valid TAX Or a Valid TAX.TYPE.CONDITION Only multi-value 1 may be used for entry

If a TAX Id is used and the TAX record has the field LINK.TAX populated then all taxes linked to the Id enteredwill be displayed using the multi-values as required, the associated percentages will be displayed in the fieldLOCAL.TAX.PERC. If APPL.GEN.CONDITION application has a record with id DIARY, then CONTRACT.GRP is identified based on theconditions defined in the fields from DECIS.FIELD to DECISION.TO in APPL.GEN.CONDITION. In TAX.TYPE.CONDITION, thetax codes that are assigned to particular groups of contract (CONTRACT.GRP) are populated in this field. Validation Rules: Either a valid TAX Or a Valid TAX.TYPE.CONDITION Only multi-value 1 may be used for entry

        Parameters:
        param - the LocalTaxCode to append
        idx - the position in collection
        Returns:
        nothing

      • setNetCharges

        public void setNetCharges(java.lang.CharSequence value)
        Set the specified value for NetCharges
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Flag to indicate whether the event is net (free) of charges. This field will dictate the way in which the foreigncharges tax on foreign charges affects the TOTAL.CASH field on the depositories. This flag does not in any wayalter the amount due to the customer. Whether or not the foreign charges tax on the foreign charges are to bededucted from the customer amount is decided by the RATE.TYPE field. Validation Rules: Only input of Y or NO allowed. If the field is set to Y foreign charges tax on foreign charges will be included in the TOTAL.CASH figureassociated with the depository. If the field is set to NO foreign charges tax on foreign charges will not be included in the TOTAL.CASH fieldassociated with the depository. Will default to NO if no input is made.

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: YES/NO/RETAIN field allowing a user to regenerate the ENTITLEMENT records for a DIARY. If this field is set to RETAIN, then the system will update the changes made in diary to all the created entitlement byretaining the details which have not been amended in the existing records.       • setRetainOption

        public void setRetainOption(TField value)
        Set the specified value for RetainOption
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: When this field is set to YES those Entitlements in which option is chose will be retained on rerunning thecorporate action service. If the qualifying nominal is not changed and it is mandatory event then the newly created entitlement recordwill be defaulted with the nominalopted by the user. If the qualifying nominal is changed and it is a mandatory event, then the freshly created entitlement will beupdated with new qualifyingnominal and the same will be defaulted in option nominal. In the above 2 cases the entitlement will be created in INAU status. If qualifying nominal is changed and partial option is chose then the entitlement will be generated in IHLDstatus without consideringoptions elected by the user in this case user have to re-elect the options. However if the qualifying nominal is not changed and partial option is opted then the newly created entitlementrecord will hold theoptions that were opted by the user and the record will be in INAU status. Validation Rules Allowed values are YES/Null only.

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

      • setSecHoldSettle

        public void setSecHoldSettle(java.lang.CharSequence value)
        Set the specified value for SecHoldSettle
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: SEC.HOLD.SETTLE will be used to control whether stock will update the SC.SETTLEMENT application. Validation Rules: SEC.HOLD.SETTLE will allow input of #145;YES#146; or #145;NO#146; only. If the ACTUAL.SETTLEMENT field on the SC.PARAMETER record is #145;NO#146; then SEC.HOLD.SETTLE will be no-inputfield that will default to #145;NO#146;. If DIARY transaction is authorised with SEC.HOLD.SETTLE field set to #145;YES#146; then the system will create aSC.SETTLEMENT record from the transaction.SC.SETTLEMENT records will be created with an unauthorised status.Thestock settlement can be recorded using the NOM.RECD.DEL field in SC.SETTLEMENT. If the user has input #145;YES#146; in the SEC.HOLD.SETTLE field of a transaction and consequently is processingthe stock nominal through actual settlement then the system will update UNSETTLE.NOMINAL field on theSECURITY.POSITION file with the nominal of the transaction when the SC.SETTLEMENT record is created. Where thesecurity position is being added to (a purchase for example) this field will be credited with the stock. Where thesecurity position is being debited (a sell for example) this field will be debited with the nominal.

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

All DIARY records are controlled by a particular security as they generate ENTITLEMENT record according to whichportfolios hold that security on the EX.DATE. Validation Rules: Mandatory input.       • setStmtNos

        public void setStmtNos(java.lang.CharSequence param, int idx)
        Set the specified StmtNos to a specific position in collection.
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: This field is used by the system in the update of the STATEMENT.NO field. As the STATEMENT.NO field is sub.valued and contain more than one set of entries - as there may be more than onedepository - this field is used in the call to Accounting to hold the STMT.ENTRY and CATEG.ENTRY IDs used in thepostings of the Nostro amount and Reallowance amount. The system automatically moves the contents of this fieldform this field to the relevent position in the STATEMENT.NOS field and is then cleared and therefore will normallybe blank. Technical note : this is done in the program SC.ENT.ACCOUNTING. Validation Rules: This is a NOINPUT field, for internal system use only.

        Parameters:
        param - the StmtNos to append
        idx - the position in collection
        Returns:
        nothing

      • setStmtNos

        public void setStmtNos(TField param, int idx)
        Set the specified StmtNos to a specific position in collection.
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: This field is used by the system in the update of the STATEMENT.NO field. As the STATEMENT.NO field is sub.valued and contain more than one set of entries - as there may be more than onedepository - this field is used in the call to Accounting to hold the STMT.ENTRY and CATEG.ENTRY IDs used in thepostings of the Nostro amount and Reallowance amount. The system automatically moves the contents of this fieldform this field to the relevent position in the STATEMENT.NOS field and is then cleared and therefore will normallybe blank. Technical note : this is done in the program SC.ENT.ACCOUNTING. Validation Rules: This is a NOINPUT field, for internal system use only.

        Parameters:
        param - the StmtNos to append
        idx - the position in collection
        Returns:
        nothing

      • setTradeOrValue

        public void setTradeOrValue(TField value)
        Set the specified value for TradeOrValue
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: This field should be used to generate Entitlements based on Value Date. For a Value Date based Entitlement, allSecurity movements that have a Value Date before the EX.DIV date of the DIARY will be included. All positions werethe EX.DIV Date is lesser than the Value Date will be ignored. If this field is left blank, the System will default to the TRADE.OR.VALUE field of the SECURITY.MASTER of theSecurity processed. Validation Rules: Optional Input. Input can be TRADE or VALUE or left Blank.

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

      • setUnfrankedRate

        public void setUnfrankedRate(TField value)
        Set the specified value for UnfrankedRate
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: This field will hold the Unfranked rate This will be a Rate or a Percentage of face value, based on whether field PERCENTAGE is set as No or Yes If not available, this will default to the dividend rate minus FRANKED.CREDIT.RATE Validation Rules Field can be inputted only when 1. CASH field for the record in DIARY.TYPE table is set to yes 2. BOND.OR.SHARE set as 'S' in SECURITY.MASTER record 3. FRANKING.CR.ALLOWED field should be set as YES at Parameter level Negative rates are not allowed. Sum of franked credit rate and unfranked rate should be equal to the rate field.

        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

      • setUpfrontPayment

        public void setUpfrontPayment(java.lang.CharSequence value)
        Set the specified value for UpfrontPayment
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Field to identify if payment is required prior to security movement. If the flag is set to YES , First Authorisation of ENTITLEMENT will debit customer account and second/Consequentauthorisation of ENTITLEMENT will perform security movement.Otherwise , Authorisation of ENTITLEMENT will perform security movement. UPFRONT.PAYMENT criteria follows below logic: If UPFRONT.PAYMENT field in DIARY.TYPE is not YES or DIARY is NO then event is not eligible for upfront payment If UPFRONT.PAYMENT field in DIARY.TYPE is YES and SC.PARAMETER is NO and DIARY is blank then event is noteligible for upfront payment All other cases apart from above are eligible for upfront payment. Validation Rules Input Allowed- YES,NO

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

      • setValueDate

        public void setValueDate(TField value)
        Set the specified value for ValueDate
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: Date the portfolios (SEC.ACC.MASTER and related cash accounts) are to be updated by the event. This is the value date of the corporate action event in respect of updating the ACCOUNT and SECURITY.POSITIONfiles as a result of the corporate action. In some cases, it may be found necessary to delay the value date forwhich customers accounts receive value. Such instances may, for example, include those cases where the dividend isreceived by cheque and, should this be in a foreign currency, will require sending for collection. If no date is entered then this field will default to the same date as that entered into the PAY.DATE field. Validation Rules: Mandatory input of Standard T24 Date format.

        Parameters:
        value - The value to set
        Returns:
        nothing

        public void setVaultUpdate(java.lang.CharSequence value)
        Set the specified value for VaultUpdate
        Throws an UnsupportedOperationException if the object is not modifiable.

        Field description: YES/NO flag controlling whether a VAULT.EXPECT record will be generated by the Corporate ACtion. Defaults to YES.If the Vault is switched off or the depository is not on VAULT.PARAMETER as being one that updates VAULT.CONTROLthen no VAULT.EXPECT record will be produced even if this field has a value of YES. Will be NO if no Securities are updated by the Corporate Action. Validation Rules: Allowed values are YES/NO only. Mandatory input. Defaulting dependant on the VAULT.PARAMETER file and theDIARY.TYPE record linked to the DIARY record.
